        <h1 class="entry-title">
         Ancestry.com and FamilySearch.org Updates and Additions to 30 Jan 2015.
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta smallPart">
         <span class="posted-on">
          <i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-calendar spaceRight">
          </i>
          <a href="http://www.emptynestancestry.com/ancestry-com-and-familysearch-org-updates-and-additions-to-30-jan-2015/" rel="bookmark">

            January 30, 2015
           </time>
           <time class="updated" datetime="2015-03-18T15:59:30+00:00">
            March 18, 2015
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          <i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-user spaceRight">

       <div class="theAuthorBox">

            <a class="share-email sd-button share-icon" data-shared="" href="http://topwebblogtips.com/why-user-experience-trumps-cro-and-seo/?share=email" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Click to email this to a friend">
             <span>
              Email
             </span>
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="share-print">
            <a class="share-print sd-button share-icon" data-shared="" href="http://topwebblogtips.com/why-user-experience-trumps-cro-and-seo/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Click to print">
             <span>
              Print
             </span>
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="share-pocket">
            <a class="share-pocket sd-button share-icon" data-shared="" href="http://topwebblogtips.com/why-user-experience-trumps-cro-and-seo/?share=pocket" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Click to share on Pocket">
             <span>
              Pocket
             </span>
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="share-end">
           </li>
          </ul>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <h4>
        <a href="http://topwebblogtips.com/why-youll-never-have-to-worry-about-another-killer-google-algorithm-update-forbes/" target="_blank">
         Why youll never have to worry about another killer Google algorithm update | Forbes
        </a>
       </h4>
       <a href="http://topwebblogtips.com/why-youll-never-have-to-worry-about-another-killer-google-algorithm-update-forbes/" title="Why youll never have to worry about another killer Google algorithm update | Forbes">
        <img alt="Why youll never have to worry about another killer Google algorithm update | Forbes" src="http://i2.wp.com/topwebblogtips.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/14253849274_ab20a010a0_z.jpg"/>
       </a>
       <p>
        As evidence of this approach, we can turn to the type of updates that have rolled out since 2012. There was the Hummingbird update of 2013, which introduced semantic search functionality to Google. Through semantic search, Google became better able to interpret the intent behind a users query, rather than the keywords of the query 
       </p>

             Record Type
            </span>
           </span>
           <ul>
            <li>
             <span style="font-size: small;">

               </span>
